<script>(function(d, s, id) {
	var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
	if (d.getElementById(id)) return;
	js = d.createElement(s); js.id = id;
	js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/es_LA/sdk.js#xfbml=1&version=v2.9&appId=200183103347113";
	fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
	}(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));

	function checkLoginState() {
		FB.api('/me', 'get', { fields: 'id,name,email,first_name,last_name,locale' }, function(response) {
		     //console.log(response);
		     //alert('Welcome, ' + response.name );
			 //alert('Your email id is : '+ response.email);

			var url = 'https://www.resultados-futbol.com/ajax/facebook_connect/fbnew.php';

			var parametros = {"id":response.id,"name" : response.name, "email":response.email, "first_name":response.first_name, "last_name":response.last_name, "locale":response.locale};
			$.ajax({
				type: "POST",
				url: url,
				data: parametros,
				success: function(data) {
					location.reload();
					FB.logout(function(response) {
					 // console.log('usuario deslogueado');
					});
				}
			});


		});

		// FB.api('/me', function (response) {
		// 	alert('Welcome, ' + response.name );
		// 	alert('Your email id is : '+ response.email);
		// })
	};

</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">
function getCookie(c_name){if(document.cookie.length>0){c_start=document.cookie.indexOf(c_name + "=");if (c_start!=-1){c_start=c_start + c_name.length+1;c_end=document.cookie.indexOf(";",c_start);if (c_end==-1) c_end=document.cookie.length;return unescape(document.cookie.substring(c_start,c_end));}}return "";}
function closeCookieMessage() {
	document.getElementById('privacyPolicy').style.display = 'none';
	setCookie('cookies_closed', 'true', 365);
}
if(typeof(setCookie)=='undefined'){
	function setCookie(cookieName, cookieValue, nDays) {
		var today = new Date();
		var expire = new Date();
		if (nDays==null || nDays==0)
			nDays=1;
		expire.setTime(today.getTime() + 3600000*24*nDays);
		document.cookie = cookieName+"="+escape(cookieValue) + ";expires="+expire.toGMTString();
	}
}

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(event) {
	cookies_closed = getCookie('cookies_closed');
	if( !(cookies_closed=="true") ) {
		document.getElementById('privacyPolicy').style.display = 'inline';

		document.getElementById('privacy-close').addEventListener("click", function(){
			closeCookieMessage();
		});
	}
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
function realpage()
{
	var date = new Date();
    var days = 7;
    date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
    var expires = "; expires="+ date.toGMTString();

    document.cookie = "iphone_redirect=true" + expires + ";domain=.resultados-futbol.com;path=/";
    window.location = "http://www.resultados-futbol.com/";

}

function mobilepage()
{
     document.cookie = 'iphone_redirect=;expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT;domain=.resultados-futbol.com;path=/';
    window.location = "http://movil.resultados-futbol.com/";

}

function select_all()
{
var text_val=eval("document.opinaform.opinion_text");
text_val.focus();
text_val.select();
}

function select_allM()
{
var text_val=eval("document.opinaform.email");
text_val.focus();
text_val.select();
}
function checkEmail(email) {
   return (email.indexOf(".") > 2) && (email.indexOf("@") > 0);
}

function verify() {
var themessage = "";
if (document.opinaform.opinion_text.value=="") {
themessage = '';
}
if (document.opinaform.email.value=="") {
themessage = '';
}

if(!checkEmail(document.opinaform.email.value))
	themessage = '';

if (themessage == "") {
document.opinaform.submit();
}
else {
alert(themessage);
return false;
   }
}




</script>
